## 1. Executive Summary

### Current State
The AI Command Center has three basic apps (Memory Viewer, Vision, Chain Runner). This plan transforms it into a full **JFDI-style executive assistant** with:
- AI-powered memory system
- Project management
- Relationships CRM
- Knowledge management
- Auto-generated daily dashboards

### Target State
A comprehensive personal productivity system that:

**Memory Lane:**
- **Extracts** memories from Claude Code JSONL session transcripts
- **Stores** them with metadata and 1024-dim vector embeddings
- **Retrieves** via dual search (entity + semantic)
- **Learns** from thumbs up/down feedback
- **Visualizes** memories in River, Heat Map, and Phase views

**Productivity Suite:**
- **Dashboard** - Auto-generated daily overview at 8:30 AM
- **Projects** - Three-tier view (Life â†’ Projects â†’ Now) with energy-based task filtering
- **Reminders** - Snooze-based system with natural language input
- **Relationships** - Full CRM with freshness tracking
- **Meetings** - Auto prep sheets and note processing
- **Knowledge** - Second-brain with auto-filing
- **Chat** - Claude Code wrapper with Memory Lane integration

### Key Technologies
- **Ollama** with `mxbai-embed-large` for local embeddings (1024 dimensions)
- **SQLite + sqlite-vss** for vector storage
- **Claude Code JSONL** session parsing + headless mode
- **React/Electron** UI with dark theme and yellow/gold accents
- **Claude Code hooks** for memory injection

---

```
  â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
  â”‚                         entities                                  â”‚
  â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
  â”‚ id              â”‚ TEXT PRIMARY KEY    â”‚ UUID                      â”‚
  â”‚ type            â”‚ TEXT               â”‚ person/project/file/etc   â”‚
  â”‚ slug            â”‚ TEXT UNIQUE        â”‚ Normalized identifier     â”‚
  â”‚ display_name    â”‚ TEXT               â”‚ Human-readable name       â”‚
  â”‚ aliases         â”‚ TEXT (JSON)        â”‚ Alternative names         â”‚
  â”‚ metadata        â”‚ TEXT (JSON)        â”‚ Additional info           â”‚
  â”‚ created_at      â”‚ DATETIME           â”‚ Record created            â”‚
  â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

  â”‚                     vss_memories (Virtual)                        â”‚
  â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
  â”‚ rowid           â”‚ INTEGER            â”‚ Links to memories.rowid   â”‚
  â”‚ embedding       â”‚ VECTOR(1024)       â”‚ For similarity search     â”‚
  â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

### 4.2 SQL Schema

```sql
-- Sessions table
CREATE TABLE sessions (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    session_path TEXT NOT NULL,
    project_path TEXT,
    first_message TEXT,
    last_message TEXT,
    user_messages TEXT,      -- JSON array
    agent_messages TEXT,     -- JSON array
    tool_calls TEXT,         -- JSON array
    files_touched TEXT,      -- JSON array
    started_at DATETIME,
    ended_at DATETIME,
    processed_at DATETIME,
    memory_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Memories table
CREATE TABLE memories (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    session_id TEXT REFERENCES sessions(id),
    type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (type IN (
        'correction', 'decision', 'commitment', 'insight',
        'learning', 'confidence', 'pattern_seed',
        'cross_agent', 'workflow_note', 'gap'
    )),
    category TEXT,
    title TEXT NOT NULL,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    source_chunk TEXT,
    embedding BLOB,
    embedded_at DATETIME,
    related_entities TEXT,   -- JSON array
    target_agents TEXT,      -- JSON array
    confidence_score REAL DEFAULT 50,
    reasoning TEXT,
    evidence TEXT,           -- JSON array
    times_observed INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    recall_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    first_observed DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    last_observed DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Session recalls table
CREATE TABLE session_recalls (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    memory_id TEXT REFERENCES memories(id),
    session_id TEXT,
    source TEXT CHECK (source IN ('entity', 'semantic')),
    similarity_score REAL,
    search_query TEXT,
    recalled_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Memory feedback table
CREATE TABLE memory_feedback (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    memory_id TEXT REFERENCES memories(id),
    recall_id TEXT REFERENCES session_recalls(id),
    feedback TEXT CHECK (feedback IN ('up', 'down')),
    search_query TEXT,
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Entities table
CREATE TABLE entities (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    type TEXT NOT NULL,
    slug TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    display_name TEXT NOT NULL,
    aliases TEXT,            -- JSON array
    metadata TEXT,           -- JSON object
    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_memories_type ON memories(type);
CREATE INDEX idx_memories_session ON memories(session_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_memories_embedded ON memories(embedded_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_memories_confidence ON memories(confidence_score);
CREATE INDEX idx_recalls_memory ON session_recalls(memory_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_feedback_memory ON memory_feedback(memory_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_entities_slug ON entities(slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_entities_type ON entities(type);
```

---

## 5. Memory Extraction Service

### 5.1 Architecture

```

  â”‚                      Entity Resolver                                â”‚
  â”‚  â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â” â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚  Two-pass matching:                                           â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚                                                               â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚  Pass 1: Exact match                                          â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚    "Amy Hoy" â†’ entity:person:hoy-amy âœ“                       â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚                                                               â”‚ â”‚

  â”‚  â”‚    "Amy" â†’ Multiple matches? Ask user                        â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚                                                               â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚  Exclude common words:                                        â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚    will, may, can, mark (lowercase), etc.                    â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚                                                               â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚  Track resolution status:                                     â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â”‚    { resolved: true/false, slug: "...", raw: "..." }         â”‚ â”‚
  â”‚  â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜ â”‚
  â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

## 10. File Structure

```
src/components/memory-lane/

â”‚

    â””â”€â”€ sessionParser.js              # JSONL parsing

electron/
```

## 11. Code Examples

### 11.1 Memory Type Definitions

```javascript
// src/components/memory-lane/utils/memoryTypes.js

export const MEMORY_TYPES = {
  correction: {
    priority: 'high',
    color: '#ef4444',    // red
    label: 'Correction',
    description: 'User corrected agent behavior',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['mistake', 'wrong', 'error', 'no', 'instead']
  },
  decision: {
    priority: 'high',
    color: '#f59e0b',    // amber
    label: 'Decision',
    description: 'Explicit choice made with reasoning',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['decided', 'chose', 'choice', 'decision', 'went with']
  },
  commitment: {
    priority: 'high',
    color: '#8b5cf6',    // violet
    label: 'Commitment',
    description: 'User expressed preference or commitment',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['always', 'never', 'prefer', 'preference', 'like']
  },
  insight: {
    priority: 'medium',
    color: '#06b6d4',    // cyan
    label: 'Insight',
    description: 'Non-obvious discovery or connection',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['realized', 'discovered', 'turns out', 'interesting']
  },
  learning: {
    priority: 'medium',
    color: '#22c55e',    // green
    label: 'Learning',
    description: 'New knowledge gained',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['learned', 'found out', 'now know', 'understand']
  },
  confidence: {
    priority: 'medium',
    color: '#3b82f6',    // blue
    label: 'Confidence',
    description: 'Strong confidence in approach/outcome',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['confident', 'sure', 'certain', 'works']
  },
  pattern_seed: {
    priority: 'lower',
    color: '#a855f7',    // purple
    label: 'Pattern',
    description: 'Repeated behavior worth formalizing',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['pattern', 'habit', 'routine', 'usually', 'often']
  },
  workflow_note: {
    priority: 'lower',
    color: '#64748b',    // slate
    label: 'Workflow',
    description: 'Process observation',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['workflow', 'process', 'step', 'flow']
  },
  gap: {
    priority: 'lower',
    color: '#dc2626',    // red-600
    label: 'Gap',
    description: 'Missing capability or limitation',
    typeBoostKeywords: ['can\'t', 'missing', 'limitation', 'need', 'gap']
  }
};

export const TYPE_BOOST_MAP = Object.entries(MEMORY_TYPES).reduce((acc, [type, config]) => {
  config.typeBoostKeywords.forEach(keyword => {
    if (!acc[keyword]) acc[keyword] = [];
    acc[keyword].push(type);
  });
  return acc;
}, {});
```

### 11.2 Embedding Service

```javascript
// src/components/memory-lane/services/embeddingService.js

const OLLAMA_URL = 'http://localhost:11434';
const EMBEDDING_MODEL = 'mxbai-embed-large';

export async function generateEmbedding(text) {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(`${OLLAMA_URL}/api/embeddings`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: EMBEDDING_MODEL,
        prompt: text
      })
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`Ollama error: ${response.status}`);
    }

    const data = await response.json();
    return data.embedding; // Float32Array of 1024 dimensions
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Embedding generation failed:', error);
    return null;
  }
}

export async function generateBatchEmbeddings(texts) {
  const embeddings = [];
  for (const text of texts) {
    const embedding = await generateEmbedding(text);
    embeddings.push(embedding);
    // Small delay to avoid overwhelming Ollama
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
  }
  return embeddings;
}

export function cosineSimilarity(vecA, vecB) {
  if (!vecA || !vecB || vecA.length !== vecB.length) return 0;

  let dotProduct = 0;
  let normA = 0;
  let normB = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < vecA.length; i++) {
    dotProduct += vecA[i] * vecB[i];
    normA += vecA[i] * vecA[i];
    normB += vecB[i] * vecB[i];
  }

  return dotProduct / (Math.sqrt(normA) * Math.sqrt(normB));
}

export async function checkOllamaConnection() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(`${OLLAMA_URL}/api/tags`);
    if (response.ok) {
      const data = await response.json();
      const hasModel = data.models?.some(m => m.name.includes('mxbai-embed'));
      return { connected: true, hasModel };
    }
    return { connected: false, hasModel: false };
  } catch {
    return { connected: false, hasModel: false };
  }
}
```

### 11.3 Retrieval Service

```javascript
// src/components/memory-lane/services/retrievalService.js

import { generateEmbedding, cosineSimilarity } from './embeddingService';
import { MEMORY_TYPES, TYPE_BOOST_MAP } from '../utils/memoryTypes';

const ENTITY_THRESHOLD = 0.40;
const SEMANTIC_THRESHOLD = 0.50;
const TYPE_BOOST_AMOUNT = 0.15;
const FEEDBACK_POSITIVE_BOOST = 0.10;
const FEEDBACK_NEGATIVE_MULTIPLIERS = [1.0, 0.9, 0.9, 0.7, 0.7, 0.5];

export async function retrieveMemories(query, options = {}) {
  const {
    entityMatches = [],
    maxResults = 10,
    db
  } = options;

  // Detect type-boosting keywords
  const queryLower = query.toLowerCase();
  const typesToBoost = new Set();
  for (const [keyword, types] of Object.entries(TYPE_BOOST_MAP)) {
    if (queryLower.includes(keyword)) {
      types.forEach(t => typesToBoost.add(t));
    }
  }

  let candidates = [];

  if (entityMatches.length > 0) {
    // Hybrid mode: entity filter + semantic ranking
    candidates = await getMemoriesWithEntities(db, entityMatches);
  } else {
    // Pure semantic mode
    candidates = await getAllMemoriesWithEmbeddings(db);
  }

  // Generate query embedding
  const queryEmbedding = await generateEmbedding(query);
  if (!queryEmbedding) {
    // Fallback to confidence/recency ranking
    return rankByConfidenceRecency(candidates, maxResults);
  }

  // Calculate similarity and re-rank
  const scored = candidates.map(memory => {
    const similarity = cosineSimilarity(queryEmbedding, memory.embedding);
    const score = calculateFinalScore(memory, similarity, typesToBoost);
    return { ...memory, similarity, score };
  });

  // Apply threshold
  const threshold = entityMatches.length > 0 ? ENTITY_THRESHOLD : SEMANTIC_THRESHOLD;
  const filtered = scored.filter(m => m.similarity >= threshold);

  // Sort by final score
  filtered.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);

  return filtered.slice(0, maxResults);
}

function calculateFinalScore(memory, similarity, typesToBoost) {
  // Base weights
  const weights = {
    similarity: 0.60,
    recency: 0.10,
    confidence: 0.15,
    observations: 0.10,
    typeBoost: 0.05
  };

  // Recency score (exponential decay over 4 weeks)
  const ageMs = Date.now() - new Date(memory.last_observed).getTime();
  const ageDays = ageMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);
  const recencyScore = Math.exp(-ageDays / 28);

  // Confidence normalized to 0-1
  const confidenceScore = memory.confidence_score / 100;

  // Observation count (diminishing returns)
  const obsScore = Math.min(memory.times_observed / 10, 1);

  // Type priority boost
  const typeConfig = MEMORY_TYPES[memory.type];
  const typeScore = typeConfig?.priority === 'high' ? 1 :
                    typeConfig?.priority === 'medium' ? 0.5 : 0;

  let score = (similarity * weights.similarity) +
              (recencyScore * weights.recency) +
              (confidenceScore * weights.confidence) +
              (obsScore * weights.observations) +
              (typeScore * weights.typeBoost);

  // Query-aware type boost
  if (typesToBoost.has(memory.type)) {
    score += TYPE_BOOST_AMOUNT;
  }

  // Feedback adjustment
  if (memory.feedback_up > 0) {
    score += FEEDBACK_POSITIVE_BOOST * memory.feedback_up;
  }
  if (memory.feedback_down > 0) {
    const idx = Math.min(memory.feedback_down, FEEDBACK_NEGATIVE_MULTIPLIERS.length - 1);
    score *= FEEDBACK_NEGATIVE_MULTIPLIERS[idx];
  }

  return Math.min(score, 1.0);
}
```

### 11.4 Memory Card Component

```jsx
// src/components/memory-lane/cards/MemoryCard.jsx

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { MEMORY_TYPES } from '../utils/memoryTypes';
import MemoryFeedback from './MemoryFeedback';
import './MemoryCard.css';

export default function MemoryCard({ memory, onFeedback, compact = false }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  const typeConfig = MEMORY_TYPES[memory.type];

  const formatTimestamp = (ts) => {
    const date = new Date(ts);
    const now = Date.now();
    const diff = now - date.getTime();

    if (diff < 3600000) return `${Math.floor(diff / 60000)}m ago`;
    if (diff < 86400000) return `${Math.floor(diff / 3600000)}h ago`;
    if (diff < 604800000) return `${Math.floor(diff / 86400000)}d ago`;
    return date.toLocaleDateString();
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`memory-card ${compact ? 'compact' : ''}`}
      onClick={() => !compact && setExpanded(!expanded)}
    >
      <div className="memory-card-header">
        <span
          className="memory-type-badge"
          style={{ backgroundColor: typeConfig?.color || '#64748b' }}
        >
          {typeConfig?.label || memory.type}
        </span>

        {memory.similarity !== undefined && (
          <span className="memory-similarity">
            {Math.round(memory.similarity * 100)}%
          </span>
        )}

        <div className="memory-card-actions">
          <MemoryFeedback
            memoryId={memory.id}
            currentUp={memory.feedback_up}
            currentDown={memory.feedback_down}
            onFeedback={onFeedback}
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="memory-card-title">
        {memory.title}
      </div>

      {expanded && (
        <div className="memory-card-content">
          {memory.content}

          {memory.source_chunk && (
            <div className="memory-source-chunk">
              <strong>Original context:</strong>
              <pre>{memory.source_chunk}</pre>
            </div>
          )}

          {memory.reasoning && (
            <div className="memory-reasoning">
              <strong>Why extracted:</strong> {memory.reasoning}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="memory-card-footer">
        <span className="memory-timestamp">
          {formatTimestamp(memory.first_observed)}
        </span>

        {memory.recall_count > 0 && (
          <span className="memory-recalls">
            recalled {memory.recall_count}x
          </span>
        )}

        {memory.times_observed > 1 && (
          <span className="memory-observed">
            observed {memory.times_observed}x
          </span>
        )}
      </div>

      {memory.related_entities?.length > 0 && (
        <div className="memory-entities">
          {memory.related_entities.map((entity, idx) => (
            <span key={idx} className="entity-tag">
              {entity.type}:{entity.slug || entity.raw}
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

### 11.5 Memory Extraction Prompt

```javascript
// src/components/memory-lane/services/extractionService.js

export const MEMORY_EXTRACTION_PROMPT = `You are a memory extraction agent. Your job is to analyze Claude Code session transcripts and extract valuable memories that will help future sessions.

## Memory Types to Extract

HIGH PRIORITY (always extract if present):
- **correction**: User corrected the agent's behavior ("No, do it this way instead")
- **decision**: Explicit choice made with reasoning ("I decided to use X because Y")
- **commitment**: User expressed a strong preference ("I always want...", "Never do...")

MEDIUM PRIORITY (extract if clearly valuable):
- **insight**: Non-obvious discovery or connection made during the session
- **learning**: New knowledge gained about the codebase, tools, or processes
- **confidence**: Strong confidence expressed in a particular approach

LOWER PRIORITY (extract if pattern is emerging):
- **pattern_seed**: Behavior repeated multiple times that could become a rule
- **workflow_note**: Process observation worth remembering
- **gap**: Missing capability or limitation discovered

## Extraction Triggers ("Surprise Moments")

Pay special attention to:
1. **Recovery patterns**: Error â†’ workaround â†’ success sequences
2. **User corrections**: Agent did X, user said "no, do Y"
3. **Enthusiasm signals**: "Perfect!", "Exactly what I wanted", "This is great"
4. **Repeated requests**: Same workflow executed multiple times

## Output Format

Return a JSON array of memories:

\`\`\`json
[
  {
    "type": "correction",
    "title": "Brief summary (max 100 chars)",
    "content": "Detailed description of what was learned",
    "source_chunk": "Verbatim excerpt from transcript that triggered this memory",
    "confidence_score": 85,
    "reasoning": "Why this memory was extracted",
    "related_entities": [
      {"type": "file", "raw": "/src/components/App.jsx"},
      {"type": "project", "raw": "ai-command-center"}
    ]
  }
]
\`\`\`

## Rules

1. source_chunk MUST be verbatim text from the transcript
2. confidence_score: 0-100 based on how clear/important the memory is
3. title should be actionable and specific
4. Don't extract routine operations - focus on learnings and preferences
5. Prefer fewer high-quality memories over many low-quality ones
6. Always include reasoning for why this memory matters

Now analyze this transcript:
`;
```

## 12. API Specifications

### 12.1 IPC Handlers (Electron)

```javascript
// electron/database.cjs

const Database = require('better-sqlite3');
const path = require('path');

let db = null;

function initDatabase(userDataPath) {
  const dbPath = path.join(userDataPath, 'memory-lane.db');
  db = new Database(dbPath);

  // Enable WAL mode for better performance
  db.pragma('journal_mode = WAL');

  // Create tables
  db.exec(SCHEMA_SQL);

  return db;
}

// IPC Handlers
const handlers = {
  // Sessions
  'ml-get-sessions': () => {
    return db.prepare(`
      SELECT * FROM sessions
      ORDER BY started_at DESC
      LIMIT 100
    `).all();
  },

  'ml-save-session': (event, session) => {
    const stmt = db.prepare(`
      INSERT OR REPLACE INTO sessions
      (id, session_path, project_path, first_message, last_message,
       user_messages, agent_messages, tool_calls, files_touched,
       started_at, ended_at)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `);
    return stmt.run(
      session.id, session.session_path, session.project_path,
      session.first_message, session.last_message,
      JSON.stringify(session.user_messages),
      JSON.stringify(session.agent_messages),
      JSON.stringify(session.tool_calls),
      JSON.stringify(session.files_touched),
      session.started_at, session.ended_at
    );
  },

  // Memories
  'ml-get-memories': (event, filters = {}) => {
    let query = 'SELECT * FROM memories WHERE 1=1';
    const params = [];

    if (filters.type) {
      query += ' AND type = ?';
      params.push(filters.type);
    }
    if (filters.minConfidence) {
      query += ' AND confidence_score >= ?';
      params.push(filters.minConfidence);
    }

    query += ' ORDER BY last_observed DESC LIMIT 100';

    return db.prepare(query).all(...params);
  },

  'ml-save-memory': (event, memory) => {
    const stmt = db.prepare(`
      INSERT OR REPLACE INTO memories
      (id, session_id, type, category, title, content, source_chunk,
       embedding, related_entities, confidence_score, reasoning,
       times_observed, first_observed, last_observed)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `);
    return stmt.run(
      memory.id, memory.session_id, memory.type, memory.category,
      memory.title, memory.content, memory.source_chunk,
      memory.embedding ? Buffer.from(new Float32Array(memory.embedding).buffer) : null,
      JSON.stringify(memory.related_entities),
      memory.confidence_score, memory.reasoning,
      memory.times_observed, memory.first_observed, memory.last_observed
    );
  },

  // Vector search (simplified - real impl uses sqlite-vss)
  'ml-vector-search': (event, queryEmbedding, limit = 10) => {
    const memories = db.prepare(`
      SELECT * FROM memories WHERE embedding IS NOT NULL
    `).all();

    // Calculate similarities (in production, use sqlite-vss)
    return memories.map(m => ({
      ...m,
      embedding: Array.from(new Float32Array(m.embedding)),
      related_entities: JSON.parse(m.related_entities || '[]')
    }));
  },

  // Feedback
  'ml-save-feedback': (event, feedback) => {
    const stmt = db.prepare(`
      INSERT INTO memory_feedback
      (id, memory_id, recall_id, feedback, search_query)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `);
    return stmt.run(
      feedback.id, feedback.memory_id, feedback.recall_id,
      feedback.feedback, feedback.search_query
    );
  },

  // Get feedback counts for memory
  'ml-get-feedback-counts': (event, memoryId) => {
    return db.prepare(`
      SELECT
        SUM(CASE WHEN feedback = 'up' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as feedback_up,
        SUM(CASE WHEN feedback = 'down' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as feedback_down
      FROM memory_feedback
      WHERE memory_id = ?
    `).get(memoryId);
  }
};

module.exports = { initDatabase, handlers };
```

### 12.2 Preload Bridge

```javascript
// electron/preload.cjs (additions)

const memoryLaneAPI = {
  // Sessions
  getSessions: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-get-sessions'),
  saveSession: (session) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-save-session', session),

  // Memories
  getMemories: (filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-get-memories', filters),
  saveMemory: (memory) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-save-memory', memory),
  vectorSearch: (embedding, limit) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-vector-search', embedding, limit),

  // Feedback
  saveFeedback: (feedback) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-save-feedback', feedback),
  getFeedbackCounts: (memoryId) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-get-feedback-counts', memoryId),

  // Entities
  getEntities: (type) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-get-entities', type),
  saveEntity: (entity) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-save-entity', entity),
  resolveEntity: (raw) => ipcRenderer.invoke('ml-resolve-entity', raw)
};

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('memoryLaneAPI', memoryLaneAPI);
```

### Task Energy Types

| Type | Color | Description |
|------|-------|-------------|
| Quick Win | Green | Fast, easy tasks for low energy |
| Deep Work | Purple | Focused, complex tasks |
| Creative | Pink | Creative/ideation tasks |
| Execution | Orange | Implementation tasks |
| People Work | Blue | Meetings, communication |
| Low Energy | Gray | Minimal effort tasks |
| Medium | Blue | Standard effort tasks |

### Project Detail View
- Planning Notes (expandable)
- Task list with drag reordering
- Phases for complex projects
- Event links for event-based projects
- Agreement/PDF download buttons

### Chat Features

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **Slash Command Autocomplete** | Ranked by most used, most recent, fuzzy match |
| **Tool Call Visibility** | Collapsible containers, status indicators |
| **Session Todos** | Checkbox task list for workflow tracking |
| **Memory Lane Bar** | Entity + semantic memory counts, expandable |
| **Image Upload** | Preview strip (up to 4), drag & drop |
| **Voice Mode** | Audio input button |
| **Remind Me** | Save chat for later (today, tomorrow, next week, custom) |
| **Pause** | Compact-lite handoff for clean session restart |
| **Quick Spark** | Fast SparkFile entry |
| **Token Counter** | Expandable breakdown (system, conversation, tools, files) |
| **Session Dropdown** | Last 8-10 sessions, auto-rename with Haiku |
| **Git Branch** | Current branch indicator |

### Freshness Indicators
- ğŸ”¥ **Hot** (0-7 days since contact)
- ğŸŸ¡ **Warm** (8-30 days)
- ğŸ”µ **Cold** (31+ days)

### Contact Fields
- Name, Email, Company, Title, Location
- Social media links
- Context (rich text)
- Professional background
- Notes
- Relationship priority (High/Med/Low)
- Last contact date

## 13. Meetings System

### Meeting List
- Organized by date (Recent section)
- Searchable by participant or topic

### Meeting Detail


### Auto-Generated Features
- **Pre-meeting**: Prep sheet with participant context from relationships

- **Automatic**: Tasks and reminders created from commitments

### Features
- **Auto-filing**: AI categorizes incoming content
- **Connection suggestions**: Links to relevant relationships
- **Tag extraction**: Automatic tagging
- **Search**: Full-text across all documents

### UI Elements
- **Background pattern**: Wavy lines (toggleable: lines/dots/crosshatch/none)
- **Cards**: Subtle borders, rounded corners
- **Buttons**: Yellow accent for primary actions
- **Badges**: Colored pills for status/type
- **Icons**: Lightning bolt, brain emoji for Memory Lane

---

### Existing Files
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `ChainRunner.jsx` | Main component with multi-agent chains |
| `promptGenerator.js` | Batch prompt generation, deduplication |
| `qualityValidator.js` | Q&A scoring (4 dimensions) |
| `ragExporter.js` | JSONL/Markdown/Text export |
| `RAGExportModal.jsx` | Export UI with format selection |
| `ragConstants.js` | Categories, formats, tags |
| `configManager.js` | Save/load chain configurations |
| `ConfigModal.jsx` | Config save/load UI |

### Planned Enhancements

| Enhancement | Description |
|-------------|-------------|
| **Semantic Deduplication** | Use Memory Lane embeddings to find similar Q&A pairs |
| **Question Type Diversity** | Track factual/comparison/troubleshooting balance |
| **Curriculum Learning** | Progressive difficulty based on previous outputs |
| **Self-Critique Loop** | Agent 3 reviews Agent 1+2 output, suggests improvements |
| **Embedding Preview** | Show vector similarity scores before export |

---

### Current Features
| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **Camera Selection** | Dropdown of available cameras, auto-selects Razer Kiyo |
| **Live Preview** | Real-time video feed in canvas |
| **Manual Capture** | Click to capture and analyze current frame |
| **Auto Mode** | Periodic analysis at configurable intervals (10s default) |
| **Frame Saving** | Saves latest frame to `%APPDATA%\ai-command-center\latest-frame.txt` every 2s |
| **Chat History** | Scrollable log of all queries and responses |
| **Claude Vision API** | Uses `claude-sonnet-4-20250514` for image analysis |

### Existing Files
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `VisionApp.jsx` | Main component with camera, canvas, chat |
| `VisionApp.css` | Styling |

### Planned Enhancements

| Enhancement | Description |
|-------------|-------------|
| **Multi-Camera Support** | Switch between cameras, picture-in-picture |
| **Object Detection Overlay** | Highlight detected objects in real-time |
| **OCR Integration** | Extract text from captured images |
| **Motion Detection** | Alert when significant changes detected |
| **Scheduled Captures** | Take snapshots at specific times |
| **Vision Log Browser** | Search/filter past vision analyses |
| **Screen Capture Mode** | Analyze screen content (not just camera) |
| **Document Scanner** | Crop, enhance, OCR documents |

## Summary

This plan transforms AI Command Center into a full **JFDI-style executive assistant** with:

### Core Systems
1. **Memory Lane**: AI-powered memory extraction, vector search, dual retrieval
2. **Dashboard**: Auto-generated daily overview
3. **Projects**: Three-tier view (Life â†’ Projects â†’ Now) with energy-based filtering
4. **Chat**: Claude Code wrapper with Memory Lane integration

### Supporting Modules
5. **Reminders**: Snooze-based system with natural language
6. **Relationships**: CRM with freshness tracking
7. **Meetings**: Auto prep sheets and note processing
8. **Knowledge**: Second-brain with auto-filing
9. **Admin**: System health, token usage, session management

### Existing Features (Enhanced Integration)
10. **A2A RAG Training**: Chain Runner with batch prompts, quality validation, export
11. **AI Vision**: Camera capture with Claude Vision API, auto-mode analysis

### Technical Stack
- **Frontend**: React + Electron with dark theme
- **Database**: SQLite + sqlite-vss for vectors
- **AI**: Claude Code (headless) + Ollama embeddings + Claude Vision
- **Hooks**: Claude Code hooks for memory injection

### Implementation Priority

```
PHASE 1: Memory Lane Core
â”œâ”€â”€ Database schema
â”œâ”€â”€ Session parser
â”œâ”€â”€ Embedding service (Ollama)
â””â”€â”€ Basic Memory Lane UI

â”œâ”€â”€ Claude Code wrapper
â”œâ”€â”€ Memory Lane bar integration
â”œâ”€â”€ Slash command autocomplete
â””â”€â”€ Token counter

PHASE 3: Productivity Suite
â”œâ”€â”€ Dashboard (auto-generated)
â”œâ”€â”€ Projects (Life/Projects/Now)
â”œâ”€â”€ Reminders
â””â”€â”€ Basic Knowledge system

PHASE 4: CRM & Meetings
â”œâ”€â”€ Relationships
â”œâ”€â”€ Meeting prep/notes
â””â”€â”€ Entity resolution improvements

PHASE 5: Existing Feature Integration
â”œâ”€â”€ Chain Runner â†’ Memory Lane
â”œâ”€â”€ Vision â†’ Memory Lane
â”œâ”€â”€ Both â†’ Knowledge System
â””â”€â”€ Both â†’ Dashboard widgets

PHASE 6: Admin & Polish
â”œâ”€â”€ Admin panel
â”œâ”€â”€ Token usage tracking
â”œâ”€â”€ UI theme refinements
â””â”€â”€ Performance optimization
```
